Instead, you just play with the circuit as you normally would, with the power on!\r\n\r\nThere are over 30 elements you can use to build your circuits. The app has everything from simple resistors, to switches, to MOSFETs, to digital gates.\r\n\r\nThe app features a multimeter that you use to probe around the circuit to instantly read voltages and currents.
